    so the test has already produced value :)

commit 6f8bf97d218569f2bdabf8f942a9b787eedafe64
Author: Vicky Chijwani <vickychijwani@gmail.com>
Date:   Sun Feb 12 06:38:03 2017 +0530

    Increase connection/read/write timeouts from 10 sec => 30 sec.
    
    30 sec is not so bad, given that we almost never block the user (except during
    image uploads). A longer timeout provides big benefits with little downside.
    There could be a lot of cases where a longer timeout would be beneficial for,
    including core user scenarios like publishing over a poor connection.
    
    Refs: #159

commit c57f64ca9e7168aa97e8c66b5fefa4fd70ad4b5d
Author: Vicky Chijwani <vickychijwani@gmail.com>
Date:   Sun Feb 5 08:44:33 2017 +0530

    Resurrect image upload code removed in commit b0c8165, because a URI cannot
    always be converted to a filesystem path.
    
    As explained here - http://stackoverflow.com/a/39490576/504611 - a URI from
    ACTION_PICK cannot reliably be converted to a URI. It is easy to observe this
    when, for example, picking a file via Clean File Manager or a Google Photos pic
    that is not already on the device.
    
    The hybrid approach should be more reliable while preserving data integrity as
    far as possible - this is not perfect but better than the alternatives.
    
    References #155.

commit a5808d044599dd87c79aa46c99a19a5c7c8dc863
Author: Vicky Chijwani <vickychijwani@gmail.com>
Date:   Fri Feb 3 04:05:18 2017 +0530

    Workaround to avoid image upload triggering spurious post conflict.
    
    This prevents the auto-save in onPause() when an image upload is in
    progress (the file picker opens a new activity unfortunately).
    
    There is no better way to handle this currently, because the PostReplacedEvent
    arrives after the activity is already gone, so the activity's Post is
    out-of-sync and hence deemed a "conflict" on the next save.
    
    This should significantly reduce the number of post conflict events seen on
    Crashlytics.

commit 9827bd5428148d366b0d176dbf664eb616f4e373
Merge: ff70392 25406dc

commit 25406dc855d7cfd6a5e02d6f53983af896ed4d8f
Author: Vicky Chijwani <vickychijwani@gmail.com>
Date:   Thu Oct 6 03:30:12 2016 +0530

    Fix #145: Users with only "Author" role are not handled correctly.
    
    Here's how role-based permissions work as of Ghost v0.11.0:
    
    There are 4 roles: Owner, Admin, Editor, Author. Each of these roles is
    effectively a proper subset of the one following it, so an Author has
    fewer permissions than an Editor, and so on.
    
    Coming to permissions for viewing/editing posts: Owners, Admins and
    Editors can view and edit ALL posts by ALL users. So Editors can even
    view and edit an Owner's posts, which is a little counter-intuitive. The
    only special case is Authors, who can only view and edit their *own*
    posts.

commit da3974b93724c942cb34dc5d7829c0e1799a2c85
Author: Vicky Chijwani <vickychijwani@gmail.com>
Date:   Mon Aug 22 22:44:56 2016 +0530

    Always update post slug when publishing a post.
    
    This is similar to Ghost's in-built slug update logic since 0.8.0
    (see TryGhost/Ghost#6631), with some differences:
    
    - The slug is updated even if a post is unpublished and then published
      again with a new title
    
    - The slug is only updated on publish, not on every save
    
    - If a custom slug was set on the draft, it will be overridden upon
      publishing
    
    Refs: #122, #130

7	3	app/src/main/java/me/vickychijwani/spectre/view/fragments/PostEditFragment.java

commit 632cb64b88cbbe5d81f35e5fea73ceff3fed0b04
Author: Vicky Chijwani <vickychijwani@gmail.com>
Date:   Fri Jun 10 03:17:55 2016 +0530

    Start new drafts directly in Edit tab + fix an orientation change crash.
    
    There was a consistent crash that could be reproduced with these steps:
    
    1. Create a new draft, a dummy post with id=0 is passed to
       PostViewActivity through its Intent extras.
    2. In the background, the post is uploaded and a PostReplacedEvent is
       fired, which also updates PostViewActivity's mPost.
    3. Rotate the screen.
    4. Delete the draft => crash!!!
    
    This happened because after (3) the Activity was re-created with the
    original Intent extras, so the replaced post was lost. The fix was to
    save the latest values corresponding to the Intent extras in
    onSavedInstanceState, and using that during Activity re-creation.

commit f49e54e3f2c1083323962c4fdc9b953421fe7d9d
Author: Vicky Chijwani <vickychijwani@gmail.com>
Date:   Mon May 18 02:45:39 2015 +0530

    Fix #63: Timestamps are always in UTC. Also improve date display format.
    
    Analysis: since we passed a custom date format to GSON, and there was no
    way of specifying the timezone, GSON assumed that timestamps would be in
    the current timezone. But that is not the case; Ghost's API always
    returns timestamps in UTC.

commit 5cc339abc71d2a1ec7188e93f24bf717970c1918
Author: Vicky Chijwani <vickychijwani@gmail.com>
Date:   Thu Apr 2 01:19:51 2015 +0530

    Refactor API calls into a separate NetworkService class, using an event bus for
    communication.
    
    This has several important advantages:
    
     - Activities / Fragments no longer have to deal with the Retrofit-generated API
    directly. This improves code clarity and ensures that the view is truly a view.
    
     - Using an event bus decouples the view from the network, so a LoadPostsEvent
    could be satisfied by a mere database query instead of a full-blown network
    request, behind-the-scenes. This lays the foundation for offline mode.
    
     - Clean code: woe to BaseActivity.sAuthToken and the Globals class!
    
     - Overall the code now probably lends itself well to automated testing, which
    is always a good sign, irrespective of whether we actually use tests or not.
